PART I : SECTION (I) — GENERAL
Government Notifications
1a- PG 6152 - 456 (01/2023) 
This Gazette Extraordinary can be downloaded from www.documents.gov.lk
ImPORTS AND EXPORTS CONTROL ACT, No. 1 Of 1969
IN terms of the powers vested in me by Section 20 read together with Sub-Section 4(1) and Section 14 of the Imports and 
Exports (Control) act, No. 1 of 1969 as amended by act, No. 48 of 1985 and act, No. 28 of 1987, I, ranil Wickremesinghe, 
the Minister of Finance, Economic Stabilization and National Policies promulgate following regulations.
Ranil WickRemesinghe,
Minister of Finance, Economic   Stabilization and 
National Policies.
Ministry of Finance, Economic Stabilization and National Policies,
Colombo 01,
January 01, 2023.
REGULATIONS
1. These regulations may be cited as the “Special Import License Regulations No. 01 of 2023”. 
2. The Schedule I of the Special Import License regulations published in the Gazette Extraordinary No. 2044/40 dated 
November 09, 2017, and as amended  and as last amended by the Imports and Exports (Control) regulations No. 23 
of 2022, published in the Gazette Extraordinary No. 2309/40 dated december 09, 2022, is hereby repealed and the             

<!-- page 2 -->

I fldgi ( ^I& fPoh - YS% ,xld m%cd;dka;s%l iudcjd§ ckrcfha w;s úfYI .eiÜ m;%h - 2023'01'01
Part I : Sec. (I) - GAZETTE EXTRAORDINARY OF THE DEMOCRATIC SOCIALIST REPUBLIC OF SRI LANKA - 01.01.2023
2a
Schedule I of this Gazette shall be inserted instead. accordingly, the Schedule I of this Gazette shall be read as the 
Schedule I of the Special Import License and Payment regulations, No. 1 of 2011, published in the Gazette Extraordinary 
No. 1739/3 dated January 02, 2012, as amended.
3.	 No	person	shall	import	any	goods,	Specified	in	the	Schedule IV  of this Gazette into Sti Lanka from any Country.
4. These regulations shall also apply to the business entities established under the Board of Investment Law No. 4 of 1978 
and subject to the Commercial Hub regulation No. 01 of 2019 published in the Gazette Extraordinary No. 2152/35 
dated december 05, 2019 issued under the Financial act, No.12 of 2012 and No.12 of 2013 as amended.
5. Licensed banks shall not; 
 i. establish Letter of Credit (LC) or,
 ii. process any payment or, 
 iii. release shipping documents
relating	to	importation	of	any	goods	which	are	subject	to	Import	Control	License	as	specified	in	the	Schedule I of this 
Gazette, without a valid Import Control License (ICL), obtained from the Controller General of Imports and Exports.
6.	 Importation	of	goods,	classified	under	the	HS Codes of 8711.60.10 and 8712.00.90 shall be permitted under Letter of 
Credit (LC) or document against acceptance (da) payment terms subject to a minimum of 180 days credit facility, with 
valid Import Control License (ICL), obtained from the Controller General of Imports and Exports.
7. a)		 Importation	of	goods,	classified	under	the	HS Codes of 8807.10, 8807.20, 8807.30 and 8807.90, listed out in the 
Schedule I of this Gazette, by any Approved International Airline Operators for the purpose of Repairs/
maintenance of Aircrafts within the approved Customs Bonded Area, on the recommendation of the Chairman 
or director General of the Civil aviation authority of Sri Lanka, shall be exempted from the Imports Control License 
(ICL) requirement.
b)	 The	recommendation	of	the	Civil	Aviation	Authority,	as	specified	in	the	Regulation	No.	7	(a),	shall	be	submitted	to;
 (I) the Sri Lanka Customs for Customs clearing purpose, and
(II) their licensed bank to release shipping documents and/or establish Letter of Credit (LC) and for effect the 
payment.

10.	Director	General	of	Customs	shall	clear	the	goods	classified	under	the	HS Codes of 0511.10, 0511.99.20 and 0511.99.30 
on	submission	of	valid	Animal	Quarantine	Certificate	issued	by	the	Department	of	Animal	Production	and	Health
11. To achieve the objectives of these regulations, the Controller General of imports and exports shall issue “Operational 
Instructions” to the director General of Customs, licensed banks or any other relevant authorities.
12.	The	final	decision	shall	be	made	by	the	Controller	General	of	Imports	and	Exports	on	any	issues	arising	in	relation	to	
these regulations.
